# UPI Error and Response Code Reference

Generated from the uploaded NPCI UPI Error and Response Codes v2.9 document, UPI Help - UDIR TSD v2.2, and Online Merchant Refund - UDIR understanding document.

## Classification rules used

- `TD` = Technical Decline. `BD` = Business Decline.
- PSP/Bank-populated response codes are normally populated in `RespCode`; UPI/NPCI-populated codes are normally populated in `ErrorCode`.
- `SUCCESS`, `FAILURE`, and `DEEMED` status usage follows the final `RespPay` result concept; many validation rows do not carry a source-explicit transaction status, so the status is marked as validation failure or N/A as appropriate.
- Common Library and PSO rows are classified as `TD` as requested.
- For source rows where TD/BD is blank or `-`, remarks call out whether the value was retained as `N/A` or operationally classified.

## API inventory and flow mapping


| PSOAPI / Layer                            | Type of API                | Domain notes                                                                                                                     |
| ----------------------------------------- | -------------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| ReqPay                                    | Transactional              | Pay, collect, reversal, refund and UPI payment flows; request message sent for fund movement and related lifecycle actions.      |
| RespPay                                   | Transactional              | Final / participant response for UPI pay, credit/debit, reversal, UPI Global and other payment flows.                            |
| RespPayReversal                           | Transactional              | Debit or credit reversal response; PSP populates same code in ErrorCode and RespCode for reversal API.                           |
| RespAuthDetails                           | Transactional              | Authentication details response validation flow.                                                                                 |
| RespAuthDetail                            | Transactional              | PSP-populated auth-detail response codes for mandate/collect conditions.                                                         |
| ReqListPsp                                | Meta                       | Onboarding/meta API to list PSPs.                                                                                                |
| ReqListAccPvd                             | Meta                       | Onboarding/meta API to list account providers.                                                                                   |
| ReqListKeys                               | Meta                       | Key-management meta API.                                                                                                         |
| ReqListAccount                            | Meta                       | Account discovery / list account meta API.                                                                                       |
| ReqSetCre                                 | Meta                       | Set credential / UPI PIN meta API.                                                                                               |
| ReqChkTxn                                 | Meta / Status Check / UDIR | Check transaction status; UDIR type BACKOFFICE supports TXN, DISPUTE, TXNDISPUTE, MANDATE, DISPUTEHIST and REFUND status checks. |
| RespChkTxn                                | Meta / Status Check / UDIR | Response to transaction/dispute/refund/mandate status check.                                                                     |
| ReqComplaint                              | UDIR / Transactional       | UDIR API for COMPLAINT, DISPUTE, REFUND, STATUSUPDATE, CHECKSTATUS and REVERSAL categories.                                      |
| RespComplaint                             | UDIR / Transactional       | UDIR complaint/refund/status response carrying CRN, adjFlag, adjCode and related reference details.                              |
| ReqTxnConfirmation / RespTxnConfirmation  | Transactional / UDIR       | Notification and acknowledgement for AutoUpdate / transaction-status confirmation.                                               |
| RespAuthMandate                           | Transactional              | Mandate authorisation response.                                                                                                  |
| RespMandate                               | Transactional              | Mandate response for execution/status/update.                                                                                    |
| RespValCust / ReqValCust / ReqAuthValCust | Meta / Validation          | PAN/customer validation flows.                                                                                                   |
| RespValQr                                 | Meta / Validation          | UPI Global QR validation.                                                                                                        |
| ReqRegMapper / RegGetAdd / ReqGetAdd      | Meta                       | Central Mapper registration/get-address flows.                                                                                   |
| ValAdd                                    | Transactional / Validation | Prepaid voucher / e-RUPI validation.                                                                                             |
| NPCI Common Library (CL)                  | Common Library             | CL embedded at TPAP/PSP level for credential/session/client-side validation.                                                     |
| PSO Token layer                           | PSO                        | Token / device-fingerprint related support layer.                                                                                |


## Error and response code master tables

### 3.1 PSP/Bank response codes - RespPay Debit/Credit/Mandate Debit and RespChkTxn

### 4.3.12 UPI/NPCI message-level validations - Online Refund Codes


| Error code / Response Code | Description                                                                                            | Error Type (TD/BD) | API / APIs involved                                    | Type of API          | Flow Name / Names | Remarks    | Transaction Status           | Section Number |
| -------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ | ------------------ | ------------------------------------------------------ | -------------------- | ----------------- | ---------- | ---------------------------- | -------------- |
| OR1                        | REFUND IS ALLOWED ONLY FOR 2.0                                                                         | BD                 | Online Refund APIs; ReqComplaint Refund; ReqPay Refund | Transactional / UDIR | Online Refund     | ; type     | FAILURE / validation failure | 4.3.12         |
| OR2                        | TXN.ORGTNXID MUST BE PRESENT/ VALID FOR REFUND; ALPHANUMERIC; MINLENGTH 1 , MAXLENGTH 35 GOING SUCCESS | TD                 | Online Refund APIs; ReqComplaint Refund; ReqPay Refund | Transactional / UDIR | Online Refund     | orgTxnId   | FAILURE / validation failure | 4.3.12         |
| OR3                        | TXN.ORGTNXDATE MUST BE PRESENT/ VALID FOR REFUND                                                       | TD                 | Online Refund APIs; ReqComplaint Refund; ReqPay Refund | Transactional / UDIR | Online Refund     | orgTxnDate | FAILURE / validation failure | 4.3.12         |
| OR4                        | TXN.ORGRRN MUST BE PRESENT/ VALID FOR REFUND; NUMERIC; LENGTH 12                                       | TD                 | Online Refund APIs; ReqComplaint Refund; ReqPay Refund | Transactional / UDIR | Online Refund     | orgRrn     | FAILURE / validation failure | 4.3.12         |
| OR5                        | PAYEE.GLOBAL ADDRESS MUST BE ACCT NUMBER AND IFSC ONLY FOR REFUND                                      | TD                 | Online Refund APIs; ReqComplaint Refund; ReqPay Refund | Transactional / UDIR | Online Refund     | ; address  | FAILURE / validation failure | 4.3.12         |
| OR6                        | PAYEE ACCOUNT DETAILS MUST BE PRESENT OR VPA MUST BE GLOBAL ADDRESS(A/C NO & IFSC) .                   | TD                 | Online Refund APIs; ReqComplaint Refund; ReqPay Refund | Transactional / UDIR | Online Refund     | account    | FAILURE / validation failure | 4.3.12         |
